// =============================================================================
// hmac_join_token.ts â€” HMAC-SHA256 signed join token utility (ADR-009).
//
// Mints + verifies opaque, time-limited tokens that grant the bearer
// permission to call `joinDecisionCircle` for a specific shop/project on
// behalf of the original customer. The token is signed server-side with a
// secret stored in Firebase Secret Manager (`JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET`) and
// verified server-side; clients treat it as opaque.
//
// Format:   `<base64url(payloadJson)>.<hex(hmac-sha256(payloadBase64))>`
//
// Payload:
//   {
//     shopId: string,
//     projectId: string,
//     originalCustomerUid: string,
//     expiresAt: number   // ms epoch
//   }
//
// Drift Â§15.1.A resolution.
// =============================================================================

import * as crypto from 'crypto';

export interface JoinTokenPayload {
  shopId: string;
  projectId: string;
  originalCustomerUid: string;
  /** Milliseconds since epoch. Tokens past this are rejected. */
  expiresAt: number;
}

/** 7 days in milliseconds â€” default TTL per ADR-009 v1.0.3. */
export const DEFAULT_JOIN_TOKEN_TTL_MS = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

const SIGNATURE_ALGORITHM = 'sha256';

/**
 * Read the HMAC secret from the runtime env. Functions that mint or verify
 * tokens must declare `secrets: ['JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET']` in their onCall
 * options so Firebase Secret Manager wires the env var at runtime.
 */
function readSecret(): string {
  const secret = process.env.JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET;
  if (!secret || secret.length < 32) {
    // 32 chars = 256 bits at 1 char/byte. Anything shorter than that is
    // unsuitable for HMAC-SHA256 in production. The check fails loudly so
    // a missing or weak secret is caught at first use, not silently in the
    // forgery threat path.
    throw new Error(
      'JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET is not set or is too short (>=32 chars). ' +
        'Set via `firebase functions:secrets:set JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET` per ' +
        'docs/runbook/staging-setup.md.',
    );
  }
  return secret;
}

function base64UrlEncode(input: Buffer | string): string {
  const buf = typeof input === 'string' ? Buffer.from(input, 'utf8') : input;
  return buf
    .toString('base64')
    .replace(/\+/g, '-')
    .replace(/\//g, '_')
    .replace(/=+$/, '');
}

function base64UrlDecode(input: string): Buffer {
  const padded = input
    .replace(/-/g, '+')
    .replace(/_/g, '/')
    .padEnd(input.length + ((4 - (input.length % 4)) % 4), '=');
  return Buffer.from(padded, 'base64');
}

function signPayload(payloadBase64: string, secret: string): string {
  return crypto
    .createHmac(SIGNATURE_ALGORITHM, secret)
    .update(payloadBase64)
    .digest('hex');
}

/**
 * Mint a signed join token. Returns the opaque token string.
 *
 * Inputs are NOT sanitized here â€” callers are expected to validate
 * shopId / projectId / customerUid via existing rule-layer or callable-input
 * gates before requesting a token.
 */
export function mintJoinToken(input: {
  shopId: string;
  projectId: string;
  originalCustomerUid: string;
  /** Token lifetime in ms. Defaults to 7 days per ADR-009. */
  ttlMs?: number;
  /** For testing â€” override the "now" reference. */
  nowMs?: number;
}): string {
  const now = input.nowMs ?? Date.now();
  const ttl = input.ttlMs ?? DEFAULT_JOIN_TOKEN_TTL_MS;
  const payload: JoinTokenPayload = {
    shopId: input.shopId,
    projectId: input.projectId,
    originalCustomerUid: input.originalCustomerUid,
    expiresAt: now + ttl,
  };
  const payloadBase64 = base64UrlEncode(JSON.stringify(payload));
  const signature = signPayload(payloadBase64, readSecret());
  return `${payloadBase64}.${signature}`;
}

export type JoinTokenVerifyError =
  | 'malformed'
  | 'bad_signature'
  | 'expired'
  | 'payload_invalid';

export interface JoinTokenVerifyResult {
  ok: boolean;
  payload?: JoinTokenPayload;
  error?: JoinTokenVerifyError;
}

/**
 * Verify a join token.
 *
 * Returns `{ok: true, payload}` if the token is well-formed, the signature
 * matches, and the token has not expired. Returns `{ok: false, error}`
 * otherwise. Constant-time signature comparison is used to defeat timing
 * attacks.
 *
 * Callers MUST additionally check that the token's `shopId` (and where
 * relevant `projectId` / `originalCustomerUid`) match the surrounding
 * request context. The verifier proves the token is unforged + unexpired,
 * not that it's the right token for this request.
 */
export function verifyJoinToken(
  token: string,
  options: { nowMs?: number } = {},
): JoinTokenVerifyResult {
  if (typeof token !== 'string' || !token.includes('.')) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'malformed' };
  }

  const dotIndex = token.indexOf('.');
  // Reject if there are MULTIPLE dots â€” the format is exactly two segments.
  if (token.lastIndexOf('.') !== dotIndex) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'malformed' };
  }
  const payloadBase64 = token.slice(0, dotIndex);
  const signature = token.slice(dotIndex + 1);
  if (!payloadBase64 || !signature) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'malformed' };
  }

  let secret: string;
  try {
    secret = readSecret();
  } catch (err) {
    // Re-raise â€” a missing secret is an operational failure, not a token
    // verification failure. Don't swallow it as `bad_signature` (that
    // would mask the real cause).
    throw err;
  }

  const expected = signPayload(payloadBase64, secret);
  let signaturesMatch = false;
  try {
    signaturesMatch = crypto.timingSafeEqual(
      Buffer.from(signature, 'hex'),
      Buffer.from(expected, 'hex'),
    );
  } catch {
    // Buffer.from on an invalid hex string can throw, OR the buffers might
    // have different lengths (timingSafeEqual requires equal length). Either
    // way, the signature is bogus.
    return { ok: false, error: 'bad_signature' };
  }
  if (!signaturesMatch) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'bad_signature' };
  }

  let payload: JoinTokenPayload;
  try {
    const decoded = base64UrlDecode(payloadBase64).toString('utf8');
    payload = JSON.parse(decoded) as JoinTokenPayload;
  } catch {
    return { ok: false, error: 'payload_invalid' };
  }
  if (
    typeof payload.shopId !== 'string' ||
    typeof payload.projectId !== 'string' ||
    typeof payload.originalCustomerUid !== 'string' ||
    typeof payload.expiresAt !== 'number'
  ) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'payload_invalid' };
  }

  const now = options.nowMs ?? Date.now();
  if (now >= payload.expiresAt) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'expired' };
  }

  return { ok: true, payload };
}

 succeeded in 1050ms:
// =============================================================================
// joinDecisionCircle â€” Sprint 4, multi-device Decision Circle merge.
//
// HTTPS Callable (onCall). Migrates a customer from one Decision Circle
// identity to another within a shop. This covers the scenario where a
// family member (e.g. bhabhi) who was browsing on a separate device wants
// to merge into an existing customer's Decision Circle.
//
// Input: { sourceUid, destUid, shopId }
// Auth: caller must be sourceUid or an operator.
// Behavior: Firestore transaction to atomically:
//   1. Migrate Decision Circle membership document
//   2. Reassign Project.customerUid from source â†’ dest
//   3. Update ChatThread.participantUids arrays
// Returns: { success: true }
// =============================================================================

import * as admin from 'firebase-admin';
import { onCall, HttpsError } from 'firebase-functions/v2/https';
import { logger } from 'firebase-functions/v2';

import { verifyJoinToken, JoinTokenPayload } from './lib/hmac_join_token';

/// Audit trail constants.
const AUDIT_COLLECTION = 'system';
const AUDIT_DOC_ID = 'decision_circle_joins';
const AUDIT_HISTORY_SUBCOLLECTION = 'history';
const SYSTEM_UID = 'system_join_decision_circle';

/// Firestore batch size limit.
const BATCH_SIZE = 500;

interface JoinDecisionCircleRequest {
  sourceUid: string;
  destUid: string;
  shopId: string;
  /**
   * Optional (Â§15.1.A / ADR-009 v1.0.3 + Codex P1-1 backwards-compat).
   * HMAC-SHA256 token minted by `generateWaMeLink`. When present and valid,
   * the token-verified path runs (existing behavior). When absent, falls back
   * to legacy SEC001 caller-uid-or-role check with a structured warning.
   * Will be required once `joinDecisionCircle_enabled` ships in Sprint 5-6.
   */
  joinToken?: string;
}

export const joinDecisionCircle = onCall(
  {
    region: 'asia-south1',
    memory: '256MiB',
    timeoutSeconds: 30,
    // Â§15.1.C â€” server-side App Check enforcement. Rejects calls that
    // arrive without a valid App Check token; pairs with the client-side
    // FirebaseAppCheck.activate() in customer_app/shopkeeper_app main.dart.
    // Debug provider tokens are accepted in non-release builds.
    enforceAppCheck: true,
    // Â§15.1.A â€” HMAC join token verification. Wired via Firebase Secret
    // Manager: set with `firebase functions:secrets:set
    // JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET` per docs/runbook/staging-setup.md.
    secrets: ['JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET'],
  },
  async (request) => {
    // â”€â”€ Auth check â”€â”€
    if (!request.auth) {
      throw new HttpsError('unauthenticated', 'Authentication required.');
    }

    const data = request.data as JoinDecisionCircleRequest;

    // â”€â”€ Input validation â”€â”€
    if (!data.sourceUid || typeof data.sourceUid !== 'string') {
      throw new HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'sourceUid is required.');
    }
    if (!data.destUid || typeof data.destUid !== 'string') {
      throw new HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'destUid is required.');
    }
    if (!data.shopId || typeof data.shopId !== 'string') {
      throw new HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'shopId is required.');
    }
    if (data.sourceUid === data.destUid) {
      throw new HttpsError(
        'invalid-argument',
        'sourceUid and destUid must be different.',
      );
    }
    const { sourceUid, destUid, shopId } = data;
    const callerUid = request.auth.uid;

    // Normalise joinToken â€” empty string counts as absent (Codex P1-1).
    const joinToken: string | undefined =
      typeof data.joinToken === 'string' && data.joinToken
        ? data.joinToken
        : undefined;

    // Hoisted so Phases 2 + 3 can scope queries to the token's projectId (Codex P1-2).
    let tokenPayload: JoinTokenPayload | undefined;

    if (joinToken) {
      // Â§15.1.A â€” Token-verified path. HMAC token verification + payload
      // binding check proves the token is unforged + unexpired, and that
      // it was minted FOR this specific request (matching shopId +
      // originalCustomerUid).
      const verifyResult = verifyJoinToken(joinToken);
      if (!verifyResult.ok) {
        logger.warn('joinDecisionCircle: token verification failed', {
          callerUid,
          shopId,
          sourceUid,
          destUid,
          error: verifyResult.error,
        });
        throw new HttpsError(
          'permission-denied',
          `Invalid join token (${verifyResult.error}).`,
        );
      }
      tokenPayload = verifyResult.payload!;
      if (tokenPayload.shopId !== shopId) {
        throw new HttpsError(
          'permission-denied',
          'Token shopId does not match request shopId.',
        );
      }
      if (tokenPayload.originalCustomerUid !== sourceUid) {
        throw new HttpsError(
          'permission-denied',
          'Token originalCustomerUid does not match request sourceUid.',
        );
      }
    } else {
      // Legacy fallback (Codex P1-1 backwards-compat) â€” joinToken absent.
      // HttpsCallableStateMigrationCaller calls without a token; this path
      // keeps mergers working until Sprint 5-6 when the flag flips on and
      // the client starts minting tokens. SEC001 + SEC002 guards still apply.
      logger.warn(
        'joinDecisionCircle: joinToken absent â€” falling back to legacy auth. ' +
          'Will require token when join_decision_circle_enabled flag ships in Sprint 5-6.',
        { callerUid, shopId, sourceUid, destUid },
      );
    }

    // SEC002: caller's shop claim must match the request shopId. Applies in
    // both token and legacy paths â€” ensures the caller's session is bound to
    // this shop even when the HMAC token isn't present to enforce it.
    const callerShopId = request.auth.token?.shopId;
    if (callerShopId !== shopId) {
      throw new HttpsError(
        'permission-denied',
        'Shop mismatch: caller does not belong to this shop.',
      );
    }

    const callerRole = request.auth.token?.role;
    const isOperator =
      callerRole === 'bhaiya' ||
      callerRole === 'beta' ||
      callerRole === 'munshi';

    if (joinToken) {
      // Token path: caller must be destUid (the joiner) or an operator.
      // The verified token is the primary authorization; this is defense in depth.
      if (callerUid !== destUid && !isOperator) {
        throw new HttpsError(
          'permission-denied',
          'Caller must be destUid (the joiner) or an operator.',
        );
      }
    } else {
      // Legacy path (SEC001): caller must be sourceUid or an operator.
      if (callerUid !== sourceUid && !isOperator) {
        throw new HttpsError(
          'permission-denied',
          'Caller must be sourceUid or an operator (legacy auth â€” joinToken absent).',
        );
      }
    }

    const db = admin.firestore();
    const shopRef = db.collection('shops').doc(shopId);

    logger.info('joinDecisionCircle: starting merge', {
      sourceUid,
      destUid,
      shopId,
      callerUid,
    });

    try {
      await db.runTransaction(async (txn) => {
        // Verify shop exists.
        const shopSnap = await txn.get(shopRef);
        if (!shopSnap.exists) {
          throw new HttpsError('not-found', `Shop '${shopId}' not found.`);
        }

        // â”€â”€ 1. Migrate Decision Circle membership â”€â”€
        const sourceMemberRef = shopRef
          .collection('decisionCircle')
          .doc(sourceUid);
        const destMemberRef = shopRef
          .collection('decisionCircle')
          .doc(destUid);

        const sourceMemberSnap = await txn.get(sourceMemberRef);
        if (sourceMemberSnap.exists) {
          const memberData = sourceMemberSnap.data() ?? {};
          // Merge into dest, preserving any existing dest membership.
          const destMemberSnap = await txn.get(destMemberRef);
          const existingDestData = destMemberSnap.exists
            ? destMemberSnap.data() ?? {}
            : {};

          txn.set(destMemberRef, {
            ...existingDestData,
            ...memberData,
            uid: destUid,
            mergedFrom: sourceUid,
            mergedAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
            updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
          });

          txn.delete(sourceMemberRef);
        }
      });

      // â”€â”€ 2. Reassign Project.customerUid â”€â”€
      // SEC003 fix: use sequential batches (not parallel) and merge
      // arrayRemove + arrayUnion into a single update per document to
      // prevent partial migration / overwrite race.
      // Codex P1-2: when a token is present, scope to the single project the
      // wa.me link was minted for â€” prevents cross-project migration.
      let projectsQuery: admin.firestore.Query = shopRef
        .collection('projects')
        .where('customerUid', '==', sourceUid);
      if (tokenPayload) {
        projectsQuery = projectsQuery.where(
          'projectId',
          '==',
          tokenPayload.projectId,
        );
      }
      const projectsSnap = await projectsQuery.get();

      if (!projectsSnap.empty) {
        const chunks: admin.firestore.QueryDocumentSnapshot[][] = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < projectsSnap.docs.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
          chunks.push(projectsSnap.docs.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE));
        }

        for (const chunk of chunks) {
          const batch = db.batch();
          for (const projDoc of chunk) {
            batch.update(projDoc.ref, {
              customerUid: destUid,
              previousCustomerUid: sourceUid,
              updatedAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
              updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
            });
          }
          await batch.commit();
        }
      }

      // â”€â”€ 3. Update ChatThread.participantUids â”€â”€
      // Codex P1-2: when a token is present, scope to the single thread
      // whose threadId equals the token's projectId (architecture Â§6.1 â€”
      // chatThread doc ID == project doc ID).
      let threadsQuery: admin.firestore.Query = shopRef
        .collection('chatThreads')
        .where('participantUids', 'array-contains', sourceUid);
      if (tokenPayload) {
        threadsQuery = threadsQuery.where(
          'threadId',
          '==',
          tokenPayload.projectId,
        );
      }
      const threadsSnap = await threadsQuery.get();

      if (!threadsSnap.empty) {
        const chunks: admin.firestore.QueryDocumentSnapshot[][] = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < threadsSnap.docs.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
          chunks.push(threadsSnap.docs.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE));
        }

        for (const chunk of chunks) {
          const batch = db.batch();
          for (const threadDoc of chunk) {
            // SEC003 fix: read current participants, compute new array,
            // write once. Avoids the arrayRemove+arrayUnion double-update
            // race within a single batch.
            const currentData = threadDoc.data();
            const currentParticipants: string[] =
              currentData.participantUids ?? [];
            const newParticipants = currentParticipants
              .filter((uid: string) => uid !== sourceUid)
              .concat(destUid);
            // Deduplicate in case destUid was already a participant.
            const uniqueParticipants = [...new Set(newParticipants)];

            batch.update(threadDoc.ref, {
              participantUids: uniqueParticipants,
              updatedAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
              updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
            });
          }
          await batch.commit();
        }
      }

      // â”€â”€ Audit trail â”€â”€
      try {
        await db
          .collection(AUDIT_COLLECTION)
          .doc(AUDIT_DOC_ID)
          .collection(AUDIT_HISTORY_SUBCOLLECTION)
          .add({
            executedAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
            sourceUid,
            destUid,
            shopId,
            callerUid,
            projectsReassigned: projectsSnap.size,
            threadsUpdated: threadsSnap.size,
            executedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
          });
      } catch (err) {
        logger.error('Failed to write decision circle audit entry', {
          error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
        });
      }

      logger.info('joinDecisionCircle: merge complete', {
        sourceUid,
        destUid,
        shopId,
        projectsReassigned: projectsSnap.size,
        threadsUpdated: threadsSnap.size,
      });

      return { success: true };
    } catch (err) {
      if (err instanceof HttpsError) {
        throw err;
      }
      logger.error('joinDecisionCircle: transaction failed', {
        sourceUid,
        destUid,
        shopId,
        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
      });
      throw new HttpsError(
        'internal',
        'Failed to merge Decision Circle membership.',
      );
    }
  },
);

rules_version = '2';

// =============================================================================
// Yugma Dukaan â€” Firestore Security Rules
// Per-shop scoping enforced on every read and write.
// Cross-tenant integrity test (cross_tenant_integrity_test.dart) MUST pass
// against this file on every PR â€” see ADR-012, R9.
//
// Sprint 1 scope: shopId scoping foundation + udhaar forbidden-field guard.
// Per-collection rules expand as Sprints 2â€“6 ship the corresponding stories.
// =============================================================================

service cloud.firestore {
  match /databases/{database}/documents {

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Helper functions
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function isSignedIn() {
      return request.auth != null;
    }

    function isAnonymous() {
      return isSignedIn() && request.auth.token.firebase.sign_in_provider == 'anonymous';
    }

    function isPhoneVerified() {
      return isSignedIn() && request.auth.token.firebase.sign_in_provider == 'phone';
    }

    function isGoogleSignedIn() {
      return isSignedIn() && request.auth.token.firebase.sign_in_provider == 'google.com';
    }

    function callerShopId() {
      return request.auth.token.shopId;
    }

    function callerRole() {
      return request.auth.token.role;
    }

    function isShopMember(shopId) {
      return isSignedIn() && callerShopId() == shopId;
    }

    function isShopOperator(shopId) {
      return isShopMember(shopId) && isGoogleSignedIn() &&
        (callerRole() == 'bhaiya'
         || callerRole() == 'beta'
         || callerRole() == 'munshi');
    }

    // Phase 1.9 code review cleanup (Agent A finding #3, my pre-flag from
    // Phase 1.2 + 1.5): the operator role canonical vocabulary per SAD Â§5
    // + PRD + Brief is `bhaiya / beta / munshi`. Sprint 1.4 rules drifted
    // to `shopkeeper / son / munshi` â€” now aligned. The `signupNewOperator`
    // Cloud Function (ships Sprint 5+ per S4.2) must issue custom claims
    // with the same canonical names.

    function hasShopId(data) {
      return 'shopId' in data && data.shopId is string && data.shopId.size() > 0;
    }

    function shopIdMatches(shopId) {
      return hasShopId(request.resource.data)
          && request.resource.data.shopId == shopId;
    }

    // App Check enforcement: callable Cloud Functions enforce it via
    // `enforceAppCheck: true` in their onCall options (functions/src/
    // join_decision_circle.ts + generate_wa_me_link.ts). For Firestore +
    // Storage, App Check enforcement must be toggled on in the Firebase
    // Console (Project Settings â†’ App Check); the rule layer additionally
    // gates writes via the shopId token claim issued through auth flows.

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Shop lifecycle write-freeze helper (SAD Â§6 v1.0.4 + ADR-013 + R16/DPDP)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Freezes ALL client writes as soon as shopLifecycle leaves "active".
    // Reads continue so customers/operators can access their data during the
    // DPDP retention window. Cloud Function 8 (shopDeactivationSweep) owns all
    // mutations while the shop is not active, including scoped deletion at
    // retention expiry. Every allow create/update/delete below AND-gates on
    // this helper per the non-optional I6.4 acceptance criterion.

    function shopIsWritable(shopId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/shops/$(shopId))
          && get(/databases/$(database)/documents/shops/$(shopId)).data.shopLifecycle == 'active';
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Role helpers (Phase 6 addition â€” aligned with SAD Â§6 naming)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function isOperatorOf(shopId) {
      return isShopOperator(shopId);
    }

    function isCustomerOf(shopId) {
      return isShopMember(shopId)
          && (isAnonymous() || isPhoneVerified());
    }

    // isBhaiyaOf(shopId) helper is intentionally NOT defined until a rule
    // actually needs to distinguish bhaiya from other operator roles
    // (currently isShopOperator covers all 3 roles uniformly). Add in
    // Sprint 3+ when S4.19 shop deactivation introduces bhaiya-only access.

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Forbidden vocabulary on Udhaar Ledger (ADR-010, RBI-defensive)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function hasForbiddenUdhaarFields(data) {
      return data.keys().hasAny([
        'interest',
        'interestRate',
        'overdueFee',
        'dueDate',
        'lendingTerms',
        'borrowerObligation',
        'defaultStatus',
        'collectionAttempt'
      ]);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Catch-all default deny (REQUIRED â€” every collection must be explicit)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    match /{document=**} {
      allow read, write: if false;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // /shops/{shopId} â€” Shop document
    // Read: any signed-in user (including anonymous customers).
    // Anonymous users don't have shopId custom claims, but they need read
    // access for onboarding (B1.1) and browsing (B1.4/B1.5).
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    match /shops/{shopId} {
      allow read: if isSignedIn();
      allow create: if false; // shops are created server-side via admin SDK
      allow update: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      allow delete: if false;

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/themeTokens/{docId} â€” multi-tenant theming (SAD Â§8)
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /themeTokens/{tokenDocId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow write: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/theme/{docId} â€” ShopThemeTokens current doc
      // Read by customer app at onboarding, written by shopkeeper settings.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /theme/{themeDocId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow write: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/featureFlags/{flagId} â€” Remote Config mirror
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /featureFlags/{flagId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow write: if false; // managed via Remote Config console only
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Sub-collections expand in Sprints 2â€“6 as stories ship:
      //   projects/, customers/, chatThreads/, customerMemory/, decisionCircles/
      //
      // Phase 1.9 code review cleanup (Agent A finding #1): the Phase 1.5
      // shared models repos target these four sub-collections:
      //   inventory/, operators/, voiceNotes/, curatedShortlists/
      // Each needs an explicit match clause â€” otherwise they fall through
      // to the catch-all `allow read, write: if false` at line 122-124 and
      // every repo call fails with permission-denied at runtime. Baseline
      // rules below honor the documented access model; per-story stories
      // (B1.4, B1.5, B1.6, B1.12, S4.1, S4.3, S4.4, S4.5) may refine.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/operators/{uid} â€” per PRD S4.1 + S4.2.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: any signed-in operator of the shop (they may need to see
      //       other operators' roles for the S4.12 Settings list).
      // Create/update/delete: bhaiya-only (PRD S4.2 AC + SAD Â§5 permissions).
      // The `signupNewOperator` Cloud Function bypasses rules via admin SDK
      // for the very first operator (PRD PQ-C locked answer).

      match /operators/{operatorUid} {
        allow read: if isShopOperator(shopId);
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && callerRole() == 'bhaiya'
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Self-delete forbidden â€” enforces the "can't remove yourself as
        // bhaiya" posture in SAD Â§6 rule table. Bhaiya can delete OTHER
        // operators but not their own doc.
        allow delete: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                      && callerRole() == 'bhaiya'
                      && request.auth.uid != operatorUid
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/inventory/{skuId} â€” per PRD B1.4/B1.5/S4.3/S4.4/S4.5.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: public to any shop member (customer + operator) â€” SKUs are
      //       the catalog and must be visible to the customer app without
      //       extra auth gates.
      // Write: operator-only. B1.5 AC #7 notes `negotiableDownTo` is
      //       operator-only â€” the rule permits the field (the model has
      //       it) but customer reads never surface it in UI because the
      //       customer_app layer filters at render time.

      match /inventory/{skuId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Soft-delete only per PRD PQ-D â€” `isActive: false` via update.
        // Hard-delete forbidden in v1.
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/voiceNotes/{voiceNoteId} â€” per PRD B1.6/B1.7/B1.8/B1.10.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: public to any shop member â€” customers hear voice notes
      //       inline on B1.3 greeting, B1.5 SKU detail, B1.7 chat messages,
      //       B1.10 away banner. The audio file itself is in Cloud Storage
      //       and is governed by storage.rules (Sprint 3+ delta).
      // Write: operator-only. Only bhaiya + beta record voice notes per
      //       VoiceNoteAuthorRole enum. Munshi cannot.

      match /voiceNotes/{voiceNoteId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && callerRole() != 'munshi'
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Voice notes are append-only per SAD Â§5 â€” no delete path.
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/curatedShortlists/{shortlistId} â€” per PRD B1.4/B1.12.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: public to any shop member â€” customers browse shortlists on
      //       B1.4.
      // Write: operator-only (bhaiya + beta can curate; munshi cannot).
      //       Finite cap of 6 per UX Spec Â§4.3 is enforced in the Dart
      //       CuratedShortlistRepo, not here â€” the rule layer doesn't know
      //       about the SKU count invariant (would require a list-length
      //       check on `request.resource.data.skuIdsInOrder` which is
      //       possible but adds rule complexity). Defense-in-depth via
      //       repo + security rule would require a future `hasAtMost(6)`
      //       helper; queued as Phase 2+ refinement.

      match /curatedShortlists/{shortlistId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && callerRole() != 'munshi'
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Soft-delete via `isActive: false` update â€” hard delete forbidden.
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // Sprint 1 stub for udhaarLedger â€” present so the cross-tenant test
      // can assert the forbidden-field guard works from day one. Writes
      // freeze automatically when shopLifecycle != 'active' per ADR-013.
      match /udhaarLedger/{ledgerId} {
        // Read: operator sees all; customer sees only own ledgers.
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (isShopOperator(shopId)
                        || resource.data.customerId == request.auth.uid);
        allow create: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && !hasForbiddenUdhaarFields(request.resource.data)
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Update: operator only + forbidden vocabulary + RBI reminder caps.
        // reminderCountLifetime capped at 3 per PRD S4.10 AC #8.
        // reminderCadenceDays must be 7â€“30 per PRD S4.10 AC #9.
        // DI005 fix: guard checks with field existence to avoid null comparison
        // failures on ledgers created without these optional fields.
        allow update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && !hasForbiddenUdhaarFields(request.resource.data)
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (!('reminderCountLifetime' in request.resource.data)
                          || request.resource.data.reminderCountLifetime <= 3)
                      && (!('reminderCadenceDays' in request.resource.data)
                          || (request.resource.data.reminderCadenceDays >= 7
                              && request.resource.data.reminderCadenceDays <= 30));
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // v1.0.4 patch â€” feedback sub-collection (SAD Â§6 + S4.17 NPS + burnout)
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Customers create their own customer_nps / customer_csat documents.
      // Operators create their own shopkeeper_burnout_self_report /
      // shopkeeper_usage_sample documents. All feedback is immutable after
      // create â€” no update, no delete. Reads: operators see everything in
      // their shop; customers see only their own submissions.

      match /feedback/{feedbackId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (isShopOperator(shopId)
                        || (resource.data.authorUid == request.auth.uid
                            && resource.data.authorRole == 'customer'));
        // Uses shopIdMatches() helper for consistency with udhaarLedger
        // rule. Sprint 2.3 cleanup per code review finding Agent A ðŸŸ¡ #1.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && request.resource.data.authorUid == request.auth.uid
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (
                           (request.resource.data.type in ['customer_nps', 'customer_csat']
                            && isCustomerOf(shopId))
                           ||
                           (request.resource.data.type in ['shopkeeper_burnout_self_report', 'shopkeeper_usage_sample']
                            && isOperatorOf(shopId))
                         );
        allow update, delete: if false;
      }

      // =====================================================================
      // Sprint A â€” 5 missing collection rules (per deep architecture review)
      // Without these, all Project, Chat, Customer, Memory, and Decision
      // Circle writes fall through to the catch-all deny and fail with
      // permission-denied at runtime.
      // =====================================================================

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // State-machine helper for Project transitions (SAD Â§9 + PRD C3.x)
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      function isValidProjectStateTransition(fromState, toState) {
        return (fromState == 'draft' && toState in ['negotiating', 'committed', 'cancelled'])
            || (fromState == 'negotiating' && toState in ['committed', 'cancelled', 'draft'])
            || (fromState == 'committed' && toState in ['paid', 'delivering', 'awaiting_verification', 'cancelled'])
            || (fromState == 'paid' && toState in ['delivering', 'closed'])
            || (fromState == 'delivering' && toState in ['closed'])
            || (fromState == 'awaiting_verification' && toState in ['paid', 'cancelled']);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/projects/{projectId} â€” per PRD C3.1â€“C3.12, SAD Â§9
      // Core commerce collection: project lifecycle from draft to closed.
      // Field-partition discipline (ProjectCustomerPatch / ProjectOperatorPatch
      // / ProjectSystemPatch) is enforced at Dart compile-time via typed patch
      // classes + CI import audit. At the rule layer we enforce:
      //   1. Identity: who is writing (customer vs operator)
      //   2. State machine: which transitions are valid for each role
      //   3. shopId scoping + lifecycle freeze
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /projects/{projectId} {
        // Read: customer sees only own projects; operator sees all.
        // BE002 fix: restrict customer reads to their own projects to
        // prevent PII leakage (phone, VPA, name) of other customers.
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                        || isShopOperator(shopId));

        // Create: customer creates draft. Anonymous or phone-verified.
        // Single-shop: removed shopIsWritable gate from create to avoid
        // extra Firestore read that can fail for anonymous users.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && request.resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                      && request.resource.data.state == 'draft';

        // Update: partitioned by identity + state machine + field restriction.
        // SEC004 fix: customer updates are now field-restricted via
        // affectedKeys().hasOnly() to prevent REST API bypass of Dart
        // typed-patch classes. Without this, a malicious client could set
        // totalAmount: 0 via the Firebase REST API.
        //
        // Â§15.1.B Triple Zero invariant â€” the close-state predicate.
        // Whenever a project transitions into (or remains in) `closed`,
        // amountReceivedByShop MUST equal totalAmount. The Dart typed
        // patches enforce this client-side; this rule blocks REST clients
        // that bypass them. Earlier states (draft, negotiating) are
        // allowed to have the values diverge transiently.
        allow update: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (
                        request.resource.data.state != 'closed'
                        || request.resource.data.amountReceivedByShop
                             == request.resource.data.totalAmount
                      )
                      && (
                        // --- Customer updates ---
                        // Customer can update ONLY customer-partition fields.
                        // Field allowlist enforces the partition discipline at
                        // the security-rule layer, not just the Dart layer.
                        (resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                         && (
                           // Customer-partition fields (no state change)
                           (request.resource.data.state == resource.data.state
                            && request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasOnly([
                                 'occasion', 'unreadCountForCustomer',
                                 'updatedAt', 'customerDisplayName',
                                 'customerPhone', 'customerVpa',
                                 'lineItems', 'totalAmount', 'selectedSkuIds'
                               ]))
                           ||
                           // State transitions: customer can commit, pay, cancel, negotiate
                           (isValidProjectStateTransition(
                             resource.data.state,
                             request.resource.data.state
                           )
                            && request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasOnly([
                                 'state', 'updatedAt',
                                 // negotiate fields (price proposal acceptance)
                                 'lineItems', 'totalAmount',
                                 // commit fields
                                 'customerPhone', 'committedAt',
                                 'customerDisplayName',
                                 // payment fields
                                 'customerVpa', 'paymentMethod',
                                 'amountReceivedByShop', 'paidAt',
                                 'paymentConfirmedByCustomer',
                                 // cancel fields
                                 'cancelledAt', 'cancelledByRole',
                                 // COD / bank transfer fields
                                 'codConfirmedAt', 'bankTransferMarkedAt'
                               ]))
                         ))
                        ||
                        // --- Operator updates ---
                        // Operators can write any operator-partition field
                        // with valid state transitions.
                        (isShopOperator(shopId)
                         && (
                           request.resource.data.state == resource.data.state
                           || isValidProjectStateTransition(
                                resource.data.state,
                                request.resource.data.state
                              )
                         ))
                      );

        // Customers can delete their own DRAFT projects (removing last item).
        // Non-draft projects are never deleted (audit trail requirement).
        allow delete: if isSignedIn()
                      && resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                      && resource.data.state == 'draft';
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/chatThreads/{threadId} â€” per PRD P2.4, SAD Â§5
      // 1:1 chat per project (threadId == projectId).
      // Metadata doc: participantUids, unread counts, last message preview.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /chatThreads/{threadId} {
        // Read: any signed-in user can read their own thread (customerUid match)
        // or operators can read all. For single-shop, any signed-in read is safe.
        allow read: if isSignedIn();

        // Create: any signed-in user can initiate a thread.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId);

        // Update: participant can update (unread counts, last message preview).
        allow update: if isSignedIn()
                      && (resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                          || isShopOperator(shopId));

        allow delete: if false;

        // -----------------------------------------------------------------
        // /shops/{shopId}/chatThreads/{threadId}/messages/{messageId}
        // Per PRD P2.5, P2.6, P2.7 + SAD Â§6 immutability rule.
        // Messages are immutable after create â€” only readByUids can update.
        // -----------------------------------------------------------------

        match /messages/{messageId} {
          // Read: any signed-in user (single-shop â€” thread-level privacy
          // is sufficient since customers only query their own thread).
          allow read: if isSignedIn();

          // Create: participant can send messages.
          // authorUid must match the authenticated user.
          allow create: if isSignedIn()
                        && request.resource.data.authorUid == request.auth.uid;

          // Update: ONLY readByUids field (read tracking per P2.7).
          // No other field may change after creation (immutability).
          allow update: if isSignedIn()
                        && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                        && request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasOnly(['readByUids']);

          // Messages are immutable â€” never delete.
          allow delete: if false;
        }
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/customers/{customerId} â€” per PRD I6.2, SAD Â§4
      // Customer profile doc created during anonymous auth, upgraded on
      // phone verification. Stores isPhoneVerified, previousProjectIds, etc.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /customers/{customerId} {
        // Read: self (customer reads own doc) OR operator (for customer info
        // display in project detail, memory, etc.).
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (request.auth.uid == customerId
                        || isShopOperator(shopId));

        // Create: customer creates own doc during onboarding.
        // CustomerRepo.createAnonymous() is idempotent via transaction.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && request.resource.data.customerId == request.auth.uid
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId);

        // Update: self (phone upgrade, profile) OR operator (display name,
        // previousProjectIds via Cloud Function).
        allow update: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (request.auth.uid == customerId
                          || isShopOperator(shopId));

        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/customer_memory/{uid} â€” per PRD B1.11, S4.9
      // Private shopkeeper notes about each customer. NEVER readable by
      // the customer â€” this is the shopkeeper's private relationship context.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /customer_memory/{uid} {
        // Read: operator ONLY. Customer must never see these notes.
        allow read: if isShopOperator(shopId);

        // Write: operator only (bhaiya + beta can write; munshi can read
        // via isShopOperator but the UI role-gates write to bhaiya/beta).
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);

        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/decision_circles/{dcId} â€” per PRD P2.1, SAD Â§5
      // Optional (feature-flagged). Auto-created on first draft if enabled.
      // Removable without affecting Project (PRD P2.1 design note).
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /decision_circles/{dcId} {
        // Read: any signed-in user (participants + operator can view).
        allow read: if isSignedIn();

        // Create/Update: any signed-in user can create (customer on draft) or
        // update (persona toggle adds participant entries).
        allow create, update: if isSignedIn()
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);

        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/golden_hour_photos/{photoId} â€” per PRD S4.5
      // Metadata for Golden Hour photo captures. Actual files in Cloudinary.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /golden_hour_photos/{photoId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/telemetry/{docId} â€” per PRD S4.16
      // Media spend counters, usage metrics. Written by adapter + Cloud Fn.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /telemetry/{docId} {
        allow read: if isShopOperator(shopId);
        allow write: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/today_tasks/{taskId} â€” per PRD S4.13
      // Per-operator daily task completion tracking.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /today_tasks/{taskId} {
        allow read: if isShopOperator(shopId);
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        allow delete: if false;
      }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // /system/{docId} â€” Audit trail and system state (SEC006 fix)
    // Written exclusively by Cloud Functions via Admin SDK.
    // Readable by bhaiya for operational visibility (admin dashboard).
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    match /system/{docId} {
      allow read: if isSignedIn()
                  && callerRole() == 'bhaiya';
      allow write: if false; // Cloud Functions use Admin SDK (bypasses rules).

      match /{subcollection=**} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && callerRole() == 'bhaiya';
        allow write: if false;
      }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // /operators/{uid} â€” Shopkeeper / son / munshi mapping
    // Created by signupNewOperator Cloud Function only.
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    match /operators/{uid} {
      allow read: if isSignedIn() && request.auth.uid == uid;
      allow write: if false;
    }
  }
}

 succeeded in 1007ms:
// =============================================================================
// shopDeactivationSweep â€” Sprint 6, ADR-013 DPDP compliance.
//
// Scheduled daily at 02:00 IST. Manages shop lifecycle transitions:
//
//   1. deactivating â†’ purgeScheduled (after 30-day grace period)
//      - Cancels active projects (draft/negotiating/committed â†’ cancelled)
//      - Freezes open udhaar ledgers
//      - Sets dpdpRetentionUntil = now + 180 days
//      - Sends bilingual (Devanagari + English) FCM to customers with
//        open udhaar + the operator (best-effort â€” see MT-2 caveat).
//
//   2. purgeScheduled â†’ purged (after dpdpRetentionUntil expires)
//      - Anonymizes PII fields
//      - Sets shopLifecycle to 'purged'
//      - Sends final bilingual FCM "data has been removed".
//
// Audit trail at /system/deactivation_sweeps/history/{auto-id}.
// Batch writes in 500-doc chunks per kill_switch.ts pattern.
//
// Drifts addressed:
//   Â§15.1.D â€” GRACE_PERIOD_MS bumped from 24h to 30 days to match the
//     SAD/Five-Truths posture. A shopkeeper who clicks deactivate by
//     mistake at 11 PM gets 30 days (not 24h) to undo before the
//     irreversible purge is scheduled. Recommended default; founder
//     can ratify or override (see docs/architecture-source-of-truth.md
//     Â§15.1.D).
//   Â§15.1.E â€” bilingual FCM dispatch added on both lifecycle transitions.
//     Best-effort: customer FCM tokens come from open udhaar ledgers
//     (the only place customer tokens currently land in Firestore today â€”
//     see drift MT-2 / Â§15.2.L tracking the missing customer-app
//     getToken() registration path). Operator FCM token comes from the
//     operators doc if present.
// =============================================================================

import * as admin from 'firebase-admin';
import { onSchedule } from 'firebase-functions/v2/scheduler';
import { logger } from 'firebase-functions/v2';

/// Constants.
const AUDIT_COLLECTION = 'system';
const AUDIT_DOC_ID = 'deactivation_sweeps';
const AUDIT_HISTORY_SUBCOLLECTION = 'history';
const SYSTEM_UID = 'system_deactivation_sweep';
const BATCH_SIZE = 500;

/// 30 days in milliseconds â€” DPDP grace per Â§15.1.D resolution.
const GRACE_PERIOD_MS = 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

/// 180 days in milliseconds (DPDP retention).
const DPDP_RETENTION_MS = 180 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

/// Project statuses that should be cancelled on deactivation.
const CANCELLABLE_STATUSES = ['draft', 'negotiating', 'committed'];

// â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
// Bilingual notification templates (drift Â§15.1.E).
// Devanagari source (per ADR-008 â€” Hindi is canonical) + concatenated
// English fallback. Single FCM payload per recipient â€” cheaper than
// language-specific deliveries; both lines render in the notification body.
// â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

interface BilingualMessage {
  title: string;
  body: string;
}

function deactivatingToPurgeScheduledMessage(brandName: string): BilingualMessage {
  return {
    title: `${brandName} â€” à¤¦à¥à¤•à¤¾à¤¨ à¤¬à¤‚à¤¦ à¤¹à¥‹ à¤°à¤¹à¥€ à¤¹à¥ˆ`,
    // "180 à¤¦à¤¿à¤¨ à¤®à¥‡à¤‚ à¤†à¤ªà¤•à¥€ à¤œà¤¾à¤¨à¤•à¤¾à¤°à¥€ à¤¹à¤Ÿà¤¾ à¤¦à¥€ à¤œà¤¾à¤à¤—à¥€à¥¤ à¤¬à¤•à¤¾à¤¯à¤¾ à¤¹à¥‹ à¤¤à¥‹ à¤ªà¥‚à¤°à¤¾ à¤•à¤° à¤²à¥€à¤œà¤¿à¤à¥¤"
    // English: "Your data will be removed in 180 days. Settle any open
    //           transactions soon."
    body:
      '180 à¤¦à¤¿à¤¨ à¤®à¥‡à¤‚ à¤†à¤ªà¤•à¥€ ' +
      'à¤œà¤¾à¤¨à¤•à¤¾à¤°à¥€ à¤¹à¤Ÿà¤¾ ' +
      'à¤¦à¥€ à¤œà¤¾à¤à¤—à¥€à¥¤ à¤¬à¤•à¤¾' +
      'à¤¯à¤¾ à¤¹à¥‹ à¤¤à¥‹ à¤ªà¥‚à¤°à¤¾ ' +
      'à¤•à¤° à¤²à¥€à¤œà¤¿à¤à¥¤' +
      '\n\n' +
      'Your data will be removed in 180 days. Settle any open transactions soon.',
  };
}

function purgeScheduledToPurgedMessage(brandName: string): BilingualMessage {
  return {
    title: `${brandName} â€” à¤œà¤¾à¤¨à¤•à¤¾à¤°à¥€ à¤¹à¤Ÿà¤¾ à¤¦à¥€ à¤—à¤ˆ`,
    // "DPDP à¤•à¤¾à¤¨à¥‚à¤¨ à¤•à¥‡ à¤…à¤¨à¥à¤¸à¤¾à¤° à¤†à¤ªà¤•à¥€ à¤œà¤¾à¤¨à¤•à¤¾à¤°à¥€ à¤…à¤¬ à¤¹à¤®à¤¾à¤°à¥‡ à¤ªà¤¾à¤¸ à¤¨à¤¹à¥€à¤‚ à¤¹à¥ˆà¥¤"
    // English: "Per the DPDP Act, your data has been permanently removed."
    body:
      'DPDP à¤•à¤¾à¤¨à¥‚à¤¨ à¤•à¥‡ à¤…à¤¨à¥' +
      'à¤¸à¤¾à¤° à¤†à¤ªà¤•à¥€ à¤œà¤¾à¤¨à¤•' +
      'à¤¾à¤°à¥€ à¤…à¤¬ à¤¹à¤®à¤¾à¤°à¥‡ ' +
      'à¤ªà¤¾à¤¸ à¤¨à¤¹à¥€à¤‚ à¤¹à¥ˆà¥¤' +
      '\n\n' +
      'Per the DPDP Act, your data has been permanently removed.',
  };
}

// â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
// Best-effort FCM token discovery + bilingual send.
// â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

/// Returns the de-duplicated set of customer FCM tokens for a shop, sourced
/// from `customerFcmToken` fields on the shop's udhaar ledgers (the only
/// location customer tokens currently land â€” see drift Â§15.2.L / MT-2).
async function collectCustomerFcmTokens(
  db: admin.firestore.Firestore,
  shopId: string,
  openOnly = false,
): Promise<string[]> {
  const base = db
    .collection('shops')
    .doc(shopId)
    .collection('udhaarLedger');
  const ledgersSnap = await (openOnly
    ? base.where('closedAt', '==', null)
    : base
  ).get();
  const tokens = new Set<string>();
  for (const ledgerDoc of ledgersSnap.docs) {
    const t = ledgerDoc.data().customerFcmToken;
    if (typeof t === 'string' && t.length > 0) {
      tokens.add(t);
    }
  }
  return Array.from(tokens);
}

/// Best-effort lookup of operator FCM tokens. Operator doc may carry
/// `fcmToken` once shopkeeper_app starts registering it (MT-2 tracks the
/// gap). Today this typically returns [].
async function collectOperatorFcmTokens(
  db: admin.firestore.Firestore,
  shopId: string,
): Promise<string[]> {
  const opsSnap = await db
    .collection('shops')
    .doc(shopId)
    .collection('operators')
    .get();
  const tokens = new Set<string>();
  for (const opDoc of opsSnap.docs) {
    const t = opDoc.data().fcmToken;
    if (typeof t === 'string' && t.length > 0) {
      tokens.add(t);
    }
  }
  return Array.from(tokens);
}

/// Sends a bilingual FCM payload to a list of tokens. Returns the number of
/// successful sends. Errors per-token are logged but do not abort the batch.
async function sendBilingualFcm(
  tokens: string[],
  message: BilingualMessage,
  context: { shopId: string; transition: string },
): Promise<number> {
  if (tokens.length === 0) {
    return 0;
  }
  let sent = 0;
  for (const token of tokens) {
    try {
      await admin.messaging().send({
        token,
        notification: { title: message.title, body: message.body },
        data: {
          shopId: context.shopId,
          transition: context.transition,
        },
      });
      sent++;
    } catch (err) {
      // Stale tokens (registration-token-not-registered) are common when
      // a customer reinstalls the app. Don't escalate; just count and
      // continue.
      logger.warn('Deactivation FCM send failed', {
        shopId: context.shopId,
        transition: context.transition,
        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
      });
    }
  }
  return sent;
}

export const shopDeactivationSweep = onSchedule(
  {
    schedule: '0 2 * * *',
    timeZone: 'Asia/Kolkata',
    region: 'asia-south1',
    memory: '256MiB',
    timeoutSeconds: 60,
    retryCount: 0,
  },
  async () => {
    const db = admin.firestore();
    const now = Date.now();

    logger.info('shopDeactivationSweep: sweep started');

    let transitioned = 0;
    let purged = 0;
    let projectsCancelled = 0;
    let ledgersFrozen = 0;
    let notificationsSent = 0;
    const errors: string[] = [];

    // â”€â”€ Phase 1: deactivating â†’ purgeScheduled â”€â”€
    try {
      const deactivatingSnap = await db
        .collection('shops')
        .where('shopLifecycle', '==', 'deactivating')
        .get();

      for (const shopDoc of deactivatingSnap.docs) {
        const shopId = shopDoc.id;
        const data = shopDoc.data();

        try {
          // Check 24h grace period.
          const changedAt = data.shopLifecycleChangedAt;
          if (!changedAt) {
            logger.warn('Shop missing shopLifecycleChangedAt', { shopId });
            continue;
          }

          const changedMs =
            changedAt instanceof admin.firestore.Timestamp
              ? changedAt.toMillis()
              : typeof changedAt === 'number'
                ? changedAt
                : 0;

          if (changedMs + GRACE_PERIOD_MS >= now) {
            // Grace period not yet elapsed.
            continue;
          }

          // Cancel active projects.
          const projectsSnap = await db
            .collection('shops')
            .doc(shopId)
            .collection('projects')
            .where('state', 'in', CANCELLABLE_STATUSES)
            .get();

          const projectChunks: admin.firestore.QueryDocumentSnapshot[][] = [];
          for (let i = 0; i < projectsSnap.docs.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
            projectChunks.push(projectsSnap.docs.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE));
          }

          for (const chunk of projectChunks) {
            const batch = db.batch();
            for (const projDoc of chunk) {
              batch.update(projDoc.ref, {
                state: 'cancelled',
                systemCancelReason: 'shop_deactivation',
                cancelledAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
                updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
              });
              projectsCancelled++;
            }
            await batch.commit();
          }

          // Freeze open udhaar ledgers.
          const ledgersSnap = await db
            .collection('shops')
            .doc(shopId)
            .collection('udhaarLedger')
            .where('closedAt', '==', null)
            .get();

          const ledgerChunks: admin.firestore.QueryDocumentSnapshot[][] = [];
          for (let i = 0; i < ledgersSnap.docs.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
            ledgerChunks.push(ledgersSnap.docs.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE));
          }

          for (const chunk of ledgerChunks) {
            const batch = db.batch();
            for (const ledgerDoc of chunk) {
              batch.update(ledgerDoc.ref, {
                closedAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
                closedReason: 'shop_deactivation',
                updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
              });
              ledgersFrozen++;
            }
            await batch.commit();
          }

          // Transition shop to purgeScheduled.
          await shopDoc.ref.update({
            shopLifecycle: 'purgeScheduled',
            shopLifecycleChangedAt:
              admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
            dpdpRetentionUntil: admin.firestore.Timestamp.fromMillis(
              now + DPDP_RETENTION_MS,
            ),
            updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
          });

          transitioned++;

          // Â§15.1.E â€” bilingual FCM after the transition is committed.
          // Note that on the FCM side this is best-effort: customer
          // tokens currently only land on udhaar ledger docs (drift
          // MT-2 / Â§15.2.L), so customers without an open ledger
          // receive nothing today. Operator tokens require shopkeeper_app
          // to register them â€” also pending MT-2.
          const brandName = (data.brandName as string | undefined) ?? 'Yugma Dukaan';
          const message = deactivatingToPurgeScheduledMessage(brandName);
          const customerTokens = await collectCustomerFcmTokens(db, shopId, true);
          const operatorTokens = await collectOperatorFcmTokens(db, shopId);
          const sent = await sendBilingualFcm(
            [...customerTokens, ...operatorTokens],
            message,
            { shopId, transition: 'deactivating_to_purge_scheduled' },
          );
          notificationsSent += sent;
          if (sent === 0 && customerTokens.length + operatorTokens.length === 0) {
            logger.info(
              'No FCM tokens available for shop deactivation notification â€” ' +
                'skipped silently (drift MT-2 customer-side registration pending)',
              { shopId, transition: 'deactivating_to_purge_scheduled' },
            );
          }
        } catch (err) {
          const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
          logger.error('Error transitioning shop to purgeScheduled', {
            shopId,
            error: msg,
          });
          errors.push(`deactivating/${shopId}: ${msg}`);
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
      logger.error('Error querying deactivating shops', { error: msg });
      errors.push(`deactivating_query: ${msg}`);
    }

    // â”€â”€ Phase 2: purgeScheduled â†’ purged (DPDP retention expired) â”€â”€
    try {
      const purgeSnap = await db
        .collection('shops')
        .where('shopLifecycle', '==', 'purgeScheduled')
        .get();

      for (const shopDoc of purgeSnap.docs) {
        const shopId = shopDoc.id;
        const data = shopDoc.data();

        try {
          const retentionUntil = data.dpdpRetentionUntil;
          if (!retentionUntil) {
            logger.warn('Shop missing dpdpRetentionUntil', { shopId });
            continue;
          }

          const retentionMs =
            retentionUntil instanceof admin.firestore.Timestamp
              ? retentionUntil.toMillis()
              : typeof retentionUntil === 'number'
                ? retentionUntil
                : 0;

          if (retentionMs >= now) {
            // Retention period not yet expired.
            continue;
          }

          // Â§15.1.E â€” capture brandName + collect FCM tokens BEFORE the
          // anonymization update destroys them.
          const brandName = (data.brandName as string | undefined) ?? 'Yugma Dukaan';
          const customerTokens = await collectCustomerFcmTokens(db, shopId);
          const operatorTokens = await collectOperatorFcmTokens(db, shopId);

          // Anonymize PII.
          await shopDoc.ref.update({
            shopLifecycle: 'purged',
            shopLifecycleChangedAt:
              admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
            shopName: '[purged]',
            ownerName: '[purged]',
            ownerPhone: '[purged]',
            ownerEmail: '[purged]',
            address: '[purged]',
            gstNumber: '[purged]',
            whatsappNumberE164: '[purged]',
            updatedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
          });

          purged++;

          // Send the final bilingual "data has been removed" notification
          // after PII anonymization is committed. Same best-effort caveat
          // as Phase 1 applies.
          const message = purgeScheduledToPurgedMessage(brandName);
          const sent = await sendBilingualFcm(
            [...customerTokens, ...operatorTokens],
            message,
            { shopId, transition: 'purge_scheduled_to_purged' },
          );
          notificationsSent += sent;
        } catch (err) {
          const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
          logger.error('Error purging shop', { shopId, error: msg });
          errors.push(`purge/${shopId}: ${msg}`);
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
      logger.error('Error querying purgeScheduled shops', { error: msg });
      errors.push(`purge_query: ${msg}`);
    }

    // â”€â”€ Audit trail â”€â”€
    try {
      await db
        .collection(AUDIT_COLLECTION)
        .doc(AUDIT_DOC_ID)
        .collection(AUDIT_HISTORY_SUBCOLLECTION)
        .add({
          executedAt: admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
          transitioned,
          purged,
          projectsCancelled,
          ledgersFrozen,
          notificationsSent,
          errorCount: errors.length,
          errors: errors.slice(0, 20),
          executedByUid: SYSTEM_UID,
        });
    } catch (err) {
      logger.error('Failed to write deactivation sweep audit entry', {
        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
      });
    }

    logger.info('shopDeactivationSweep: sweep complete', {
      transitioned,
      purged,
      projectsCancelled,
      ledgersFrozen,
      notificationsSent,
      errorCount: errors.length,
    });
  },
);

+    // both token and legacy paths — ensures the caller's session is bound to

+// =============================================================================
+// hmac_join_token.ts — HMAC-SHA256 signed join token utility (ADR-009).
+//
+// Mints + verifies opaque, time-limited tokens that grant the bearer
+// permission to call `joinDecisionCircle` for a specific shop/project on
+// behalf of the original customer. The token is signed server-side with a
+// secret stored in Firebase Secret Manager (`JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET`) and
+// verified server-side; clients treat it as opaque.
+//
+// Format:   `<base64url(payloadJson)>.<hex(hmac-sha256(payloadBase64))>`
+//
+// Payload:
+//   {
+//     shopId: string,
+//     projectId: string,
+//     originalCustomerUid: string,
+//     expiresAt: number   // ms epoch
+//   }
+//
+// Drift §15.1.A resolution.
+// =============================================================================
+
+import * as crypto from 'crypto';
+
+export interface JoinTokenPayload {
+  shopId: string;
+  projectId: string;
+  originalCustomerUid: string;
+  /** Milliseconds since epoch. Tokens past this are rejected. */
+  expiresAt: number;
+}
+
+/** 7 days in milliseconds — default TTL per ADR-009 v1.0.3. */
+export const DEFAULT_JOIN_TOKEN_TTL_MS = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
+
+const SIGNATURE_ALGORITHM = 'sha256';
+
+/**
+ * Read the HMAC secret from the runtime env. Functions that mint or verify
+ * tokens must declare `secrets: ['JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET']` in their onCall
+ * options so Firebase Secret Manager wires the env var at runtime.
+ */
+function readSecret(): string {
+  const secret = process.env.JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET;
+  if (!secret || secret.length < 32) {
+    // 32 chars = 256 bits at 1 char/byte. Anything shorter than that is
+    // unsuitable for HMAC-SHA256 in production. The check fails loudly so
+    // a missing or weak secret is caught at first use, not silently in the
+    // forgery threat path.
+    throw new Error(
+      'JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET is not set or is too short (>=32 chars). ' +
+        'Set via `firebase functions:secrets:set JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET` per ' +
+        'docs/runbook/staging-setup.md.',
+    );
+  }
+  return secret;
+}
+
+function base64UrlEncode(input: Buffer | string): string {
+  const buf = typeof input === 'string' ? Buffer.from(input, 'utf8') : input;
+  return buf
+    .toString('base64')
+    .replace(/\+/g, '-')
+    .replace(/\//g, '_')
+    .replace(/=+$/, '');
+}
+
+function base64UrlDecode(input: string): Buffer {
+  const padded = input
+    .replace(/-/g, '+')
+    .replace(/_/g, '/')
+    .padEnd(input.length + ((4 - (input.length % 4)) % 4), '=');
+  return Buffer.from(padded, 'base64');
+}
+
+function signPayload(payloadBase64: string, secret: string): string {
+  return crypto
+    .createHmac(SIGNATURE_ALGORITHM, secret)
+    .update(payloadBase64)
+    .digest('hex');
+}
+
+/**
+ * Mint a signed join token. Returns the opaque token string.
+ *
+ * Inputs are NOT sanitized here — callers are expected to validate
+ * shopId / projectId / customerUid via existing rule-layer or callable-input
+ * gates before requesting a token.
+ */
+export function mintJoinToken(input: {
+  shopId: string;
+  projectId: string;
+  originalCustomerUid: string;
+  /** Token lifetime in ms. Defaults to 7 days per ADR-009. */
+  ttlMs?: number;
+  /** For testing — override the "now" reference. */
+  nowMs?: number;
+}): string {
+  const now = input.nowMs ?? Date.now();
+  const ttl = input.ttlMs ?? DEFAULT_JOIN_TOKEN_TTL_MS;
+  const payload: JoinTokenPayload = {
+    shopId: input.shopId,
+    projectId: input.projectId,
+    originalCustomerUid: input.originalCustomerUid,
+    expiresAt: now + ttl,
+  };
+  const payloadBase64 = base64UrlEncode(JSON.stringify(payload));
+  const signature = signPayload(payloadBase64, readSecret());
+  return `${payloadBase64}.${signature}`;
+}
+
+export type JoinTokenVerifyError =
+  | 'malformed'
+  | 'bad_signature'
+  | 'expired'
+  | 'payload_invalid';
+
+export interface JoinTokenVerifyResult {
+  ok: boolean;
+  payload?: JoinTokenPayload;
+  error?: JoinTokenVerifyError;
+}
+
+/**
+ * Verify a join token.
+ *
+ * Returns `{ok: true, payload}` if the token is well-formed, the signature
+ * matches, and the token has not expired. Returns `{ok: false, error}`
+ * otherwise. Constant-time signature comparison is used to defeat timing
+ * attacks.
+ *
+ * Callers MUST additionally check that the token's `shopId` (and where
+ * relevant `projectId` / `originalCustomerUid`) match the surrounding
+ * request context. The verifier proves the token is unforged + unexpired,
+ * not that it's the right token for this request.
+ */
+export function verifyJoinToken(
+  token: string,
+  options: { nowMs?: number } = {},
+): JoinTokenVerifyResult {
+  if (typeof token !== 'string' || !token.includes('.')) {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'malformed' };
+  }
+
+  const dotIndex = token.indexOf('.');
+  // Reject if there are MULTIPLE dots — the format is exactly two segments.
+  if (token.lastIndexOf('.') !== dotIndex) {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'malformed' };
+  }
+  const payloadBase64 = token.slice(0, dotIndex);
+  const signature = token.slice(dotIndex + 1);
+  if (!payloadBase64 || !signature) {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'malformed' };
+  }
+
+  let secret: string;
+  try {
+    secret = readSecret();
+  } catch (err) {
+    // Re-raise — a missing secret is an operational failure, not a token
+    // verification failure. Don't swallow it as `bad_signature` (that
+    // would mask the real cause).
+    throw err;
+  }
+
+  const expected = signPayload(payloadBase64, secret);
+  let signaturesMatch = false;
+  try {
+    signaturesMatch = crypto.timingSafeEqual(
+      Buffer.from(signature, 'hex'),
+      Buffer.from(expected, 'hex'),
+    );
+  } catch {
+    // Buffer.from on an invalid hex string can throw, OR the buffers might
+    // have different lengths (timingSafeEqual requires equal length). Either
+    // way, the signature is bogus.
+    return { ok: false, error: 'bad_signature' };
+  }
+  if (!signaturesMatch) {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'bad_signature' };
+  }
+
+  let payload: JoinTokenPayload;
+  try {
+    const decoded = base64UrlDecode(payloadBase64).toString('utf8');
+    payload = JSON.parse(decoded) as JoinTokenPayload;
+  } catch {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'payload_invalid' };
+  }
+  if (
+    typeof payload.shopId !== 'string' ||
+    typeof payload.projectId !== 'string' ||
+    typeof payload.originalCustomerUid !== 'string' ||
+    typeof payload.expiresAt !== 'number'
+  ) {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'payload_invalid' };
+  }
+
+  const now = options.nowMs ?? Date.now();
+  if (now >= payload.expiresAt) {
+    return { ok: false, error: 'expired' };
+  }
+
+  return { ok: true, payload };
+}

// =============================================================================
// join_decision_circle.test.ts â€” joinToken backwards-compat (Codex P1-1).
//
// Validates that joinDecisionCircle accepts calls without a joinToken via the
// legacy SEC001 caller-uid-or-role fallback path, while still enforcing the
// token-verified path when a token IS provided.
//
// Coverage:
//   1. Fallback path: sourceUid caller, no joinToken â†’ succeeds + warn logged
//   2. Fallback path: operator caller, no joinToken â†’ succeeds + warn logged
//   3. Fallback path: unauthorized caller (not sourceUid/operator), no joinToken
//      â†’ permission-denied
//   4. Token path: valid token + destUid caller â†’ succeeds, verify called, no warn
//   5. Token path: invalid token â†’ permission-denied

  HttpsError: class extends Error {
    code: string;

  },
